<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3119_53d082-f1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-video"><video height="1080" style="aspect-ratio: 1920 / 1080;" width="1920" autoplay="" loop="" muted="" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/250915_flaconi_CompanyVideo2526_V05_FINAL_HighRes.mp4"></video></figure>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3119_966b75-4d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-row kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3119_835956-92"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3119_4ac7e5-d3 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3119_18d803-76"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left">Welcome to flaconi!</h1>



<p class="has-text-align-left"><strong>We don’t just sell beauty products —<br>we engineer beautiful shopping experiences.</strong></p>



<p class="has-text-align-left">Since 2011, flaconi has blended dynamic tech innovation with the world of premium beauty. Based in Berlin, we are a leading player in the industry, driven by around 700 colleagues from over 60 nations.</p>



<p>We are always on the lookout for passionate talents ready to shape the future of the beauty tech industry with us. Join our creative, international, and fast-paced environment where teamwork and innovation define our daily work.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-left">Ready to revolutionize the beauty industry with us? Become part of a success story that goes far beyond traditional retail!</p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3119_fe6854-50"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><a href="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/en/stellenangebote/"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="265" height="239" src="https://www.flaconi.de/karriere/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/explore.png" alt="" class="wp-image-4797"></a></figure>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3119_bd65fa-59"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3119_ba8e3c-2d alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-two-grid kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column3119_442669-20"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3119_d971bc-a3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3119_d971bc-a3">Locations</h2>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id3119_ba39af-52 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-row kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kt-inner-column-height-full kb-theme-content-width">

<p class="kt-adv-heading3119_57662c-76 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3119_57662c-76"><strong>Headquarters</strong></p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading3119_d635f7-2f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3119_d635f7-2f"><strong>Berlin</strong></p>



<p>Our modern, seven-story HQ “The Benjamin” is located in Berlin-Charlottenburg. With beautiful views of the Spree River, it’s a premier facility built for your success.</p>



<p>We designed this workspace to facilitate interaction, collaboration, and creativity, ensuring you have everything you need to make an impact.</p>



<p>Check out all open positions at flaconi’s Berlin headquarters below.</p>

<p class="kt-adv-heading3119_3b39a5-c8 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3119_3b39a5-c8"><strong>Logistics Center</strong></p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading3119_880a29-ae wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3119_880a29-ae"><strong>Halle (Saale)</strong></p>



<p>Our logistics center “Polarstern” is where our entire logistics process—from picking to shipping—comes to life.</p>



<p>This is a truly special workplace, blending high-tech innovation with the expertise of our logistics team. If you thrive in a modern, fast-growing environment, you’ll fit right in.</p>



<p>Join us and start your flaconi journey – explore our job openings in Halle and become part of our logistics team!</p>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading3119_426ede-d3 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading3119_426ede-d3">flaconi Culture</h2>



<p>The culture of a company is what truly defines it. Sure, there are many other companies selling beauty products and numerous online shops – but there’s only one flaconi! We take pride in the culture we have built, which is shaped by three essential elements:</p>



<p><strong>Code of Ethics</strong> | <strong>Values </strong>| <strong>Leadership Standards</strong></p>
